<p>First attested in the 1950s, becoming common in the late 1970s. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дезинформа́ция</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dezinformácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">désinformation</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">des-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:informatie.html>informatie</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dessert.html>dessert</a> (7449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:dessert.html>dessert</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">desservir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">disserve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">dés-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dis-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">servir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">serve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thus literally meaning “removal of what <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> served”.
</p>

<ol><li>then (at that time)
<dl><dd><i>Vollenhove <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> in 936 <a href = vnd.unilang:vermeld.html>vermeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> 'Fulnaho'. <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebied.html>gebied</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:destijds.html>destijds</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woud.html>woud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigendom.html>eigendom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:otto.html>Otto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>Grote</a>.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/VollenhoveGeschiedenis">[1]</a></sup>  |  Vollenhove <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> already in 936 mentioned as 'Fulnaho'. The region <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> at that time a forest that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the property of <a href = vnd.unilang:otto.html>Otto</a> the Great.</dd></dl></li></ol>

***deuce.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deuce.html>deuce</a> (17222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">dewes</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">duo</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:deuce.html>deuce</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:deuces.html>deuces</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A card with two <a href = vnd.unilang:pips.html>pips</a>, one of four in a standard deck of playing cards.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dice games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A side of a <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> with two <a href = vnd.unilang:spots.html>spots</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dice games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cast of dice totalling two.</li>
<li>The number two.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">tennis</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tied game where either player can win by scoring two consecutive points.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">baseball</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A curveball.</li>
<li>A '32 <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ford" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ford">Ford</a>.
<ul><li><b>1978</b>, Mayall, <a href = vnd.unilang:joe.html>Joe</a>. "Driving Impression: Reproduction <b><a href = vnd.unilang:deuce.html>Deuce</a></b> Hiboy", in <i>Rod Action</i>, p.26</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> 2-barrel (twin choke) carburetors <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in the phrase <i>3 <a href = vnd.unilang:deuces.html>deuces</a></i>: an arrangement on a common intake manifold</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:restaurants.html>restaurants</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A table seating two <a href = vnd.unilang:diners.html>diners</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Canada, US<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of excrement.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">piece of <a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <i>See</i> Thesaurus:defecation</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dusius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">phantom, specter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scottish_Gaelic" class="extiw" title="w:Scottish Gaelic">Scottish Gaelic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gd">taibhs</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gd">taibhse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">apparition, ghost</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></i> (compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deity</i>).

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">epithet</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The Devil, <span class="use-with-mention">used in exclamations of confusion or anger.</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deugd.html>deugd</a> (6578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dōghet</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dōget</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dugath</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dugeth</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dugith</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">virtue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dugunþō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">usefulness, virtue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰewgʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be ready, be sufficient</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***deugniet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deugniet.html>deugniet</a> (20355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deugen.html>deugen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be good</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; parallel to cognate <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Taugenichts</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">døgenigt</i> (the latter of which <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> on a somewhat different sense).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deugniet.html>deugniet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deugnieten.html>deugnieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deugnietje.html>deugnietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(originally) good-for-nothing</li>
<li>(usually) <a href = vnd.unilang:rascal.html>rascal</a>, scamp, a naughty boy</li>
<li>(term of <a href = vnd.unilang:endearment.html>endearment</a>) knave, amusing boy</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a> (76453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Galician-Portuguese" class="extiw" title="w:Galician-Portuguese">Old Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="roa-opt"><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a>, deity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, unusual in that it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> derived from the nominative instead of class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*deiwos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a>, deity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*deywós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a>, deity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dyew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sky, heaven</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">devise</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">devise</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">devise</i>. The financial senses <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Devise</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">devise</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:devotie.html>devotie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">devotion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dēvōtiō</i>.

<li>an act of worship, a religious mass or service</li></ol>

***diaken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diaken</a> (23198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diaken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ecclesiastical_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Ecclesiastical Latin">Ecclesiastical Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">diaconus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">διᾱ́κονος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">diā́konos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">servant, minister</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diaken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diakenen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diakens.html>diakens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:diaken.html>diakentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">diacones</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Protestantism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deacon, person involved in an ecclesiastical lay office for social affairs and charity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Roman Catholicism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deacon, male in an unordained clerical office qualified for parish work</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deken.html>deken</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">diaconie</span></li></ul>
